	<body>
		<category name="Shield Capacity Buff Uncapper">
			<comment>Percentage-based buffs to shield capacity (like from skills or relics) </comment>
			<comment>have a cap imposed on them, that prevents the bonus from exceeding a certain amount.</comment>
			<comment>This number's actually a bit low, and most shields of green or higher rarity will end up not getting the full effect they should.</comment>
			<comment>This mod removes that cap.</comment>
			<comment>Some of this mod's statements conflict with UCP, so I've merged the conflicting statements into optional compatibility versions.</comment>
			<comment></comment>
			<comment>Many thanks to apple1417 for helping me figure out all the math behind this.</comment>
			<category name="Amplify Shields" MUT="true">
